 3172 
 3173 ## Character mappings common to (non-extended) Big5
 3174 ## and Big5-HKSCS
 3175 ##
 3176 ## Some mappings for non-Hanzi characters
 3177 ## particularly 0xC6XX and 0xC77 ranges within 
 3178 ## the non-extended version of Big5 have redefined
 3179 ## mappings within Big5-HKSCS and are therefore�
 3180 ## excluded from the tested Big5 subset below
 3181 ## For example  0xC7B3 <-> U+0401  # CYRILLIC CAPITAL LETTER IO (Big5)
 3182 ##              0xC7B3 <-> U+30B7  # KATAKANA LETTER SI (Big5-HKSCS (1999 & 2001 versions))
 3183 ##
